## <a name="about-coremark"></a><span data-ttu-id="c5885-2376">About CoreMark</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c5885-2376">About CoreMark</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="c5885-2377">Linux numbers were computed by running [CoreMark](http://www.eembc.org/coremark/faq.php) on Ubuntu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c5885-2377">Linux numbers were computed by running [CoreMark](http://www.eembc.org/coremark/faq.php) on Ubuntu.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c5885-2378">CoreMark was configured with the number of threads set to the number of virtual CPUs, and concurrency set to PThreads.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c5885-2378">CoreMark was configured with the number of threads set to the number of virtual CPUs, and concurrency set to PThreads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c5885-2379">The target number of iterations was adjusted based on expected performance to provide a runtime of at least 20 seconds (typically much longer).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c5885-2379">The target number of iterations was adjusted based on expected performance to provide a runtime of at least 20 seconds (typically much longer).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c5885-2380">The final score represents the number of iterations completed divided by the number of seconds it took to run the test.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c5885-2380">The final score represents the number of iterations completed divided by the number of seconds it took to run the test.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c5885-2381">Each test was run at least seven times on each VM.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c5885-2381">Each test was run at least seven times on each VM.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c5885-2382">Test run dates shown above.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c5885-2382">Test run dates shown above.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c5885-2383">Tests run on multiple VMs across Azure public regions the VM was supported in on the date run.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c5885-2383">Tests run on multiple VMs across Azure public regions the VM was supported in on the date run.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c5885-2384">Basic A and B (Burstable) series not shown because performance is variable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c5885-2384">Basic A and B (Burstable) series not shown because performance is variable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c5885-2385">N
